static __inline__ int major(dev_t _dev)
{
  return (_dev >> 8) & 0xfff;
}

static __inline__ int minor(dev_t _dev)
{
  return (_dev & 0xff) | ((_dev >> 12) & 0xfff00);
}

static __inline__ dev_t makedev(int __ma, int __mi)
{
  return ((__ma & 0xfff) << 8) | (__mi & 0xff) | ((__mi & 0xfff00) << 12);
}

# 48 "/mnt/data/Projects/bdclient/coverage/pin-3.21-98484-ge7cd811fd-gcc-linux/extras/crt/include/os-apis/signals-core.h" 3 4
static inline void OS_SigSetAdd(SIGSET_T* set, int signal)
{
    UINT64 mask = (UINT64)1 << (signal - 1);
    *set |= mask;
}
# 61 "/mnt/data/Projects/bdclient/coverage/pin-3.21-98484-ge7cd811fd-gcc-linux/extras/crt/include/os-apis/signals-core.h" 3 4
static inline int OS_SigSetIsMember(const SIGSET_T* set, int signal)
{
    UINT64 mask = (UINT64)1 << (signal - 1);
    return ((*set & mask) != 0);
}

static inline void OS_SigSetFill(SIGSET_T* set) { *set = (8 == sizeof(SIGSET_T)) ? ~(UINT64)0 : ~(UINT32)0; }







static inline void OS_SigSetRemove(SIGSET_T* set, int signal)
{
    UINT64 mask = (UINT64)1 << (signal - 1);
    *set &= ~mask;
}

   int8_t s_byte[2];

   uint8_t byte[4];
   uint16_t word[2];
   int8_t s_byte[4];
   int16_t s_word[2];

  struct {
    uint8_t b0;
    uint8_t b1;
    uint8_t b2;
    uint8_t b3;
  } b;

    uint16_t w0;
    uint16_t w1;
  } w;

} xed_union32_t ;

    uint16_t w2;
    uint16_t w3;
  } w;
  struct {
    uint32_t lo32;

  } s;
    uint64_t u64;
    int64_t i64;
} xed_union64_t ;

static inline uint64_t xed_make_uint64(uint32_t hi, uint32_t lo) {
    xed_union64_t y;
    y.s.lo32= lo;
    y.s.hi32= hi;
    return y.u64;
}
static inline int64_t xed_make_int64(uint32_t hi, uint32_t lo) {
    xed_union64_t y;
    y.s.lo32= lo;
    y.s.hi32= hi;
    return y.i64;
}

static inline void xed_state_init2(xed_state_t* p,
                                      xed_machine_mode_enum_t arg_mmode,
                                      xed_address_width_enum_t arg_stack_addr_width) {
    p->mmode=arg_mmode;
    p->stack_addr_width=arg_stack_addr_width;

static inline void xed_state_zero(xed_state_t* p) {
    p->mmode= XED_MACHINE_MODE_INVALID;
    p->stack_addr_width=XED_ADDRESS_WIDTH_INVALID;
}







static inline xed_machine_mode_enum_t xed_state_get_machine_mode(const xed_state_t* p) {
    return p->mmode;
}




static inline xed_bool_t xed_state_long64_mode(const xed_state_t* p) {
    return xed_state_get_machine_mode(p) == XED_MACHINE_MODE_LONG_64;
}


static inline xed_bool_t xed_state_real_mode(const xed_state_t* p) {
    xed_machine_mode_enum_t mmode = xed_state_get_machine_mode(p);
    return ( mmode == XED_MACHINE_MODE_REAL_16 ||
             mmode == XED_MACHINE_MODE_REAL_32 );
}


static inline xed_bool_t xed_state_mode_width_16(const xed_state_t* p) {
    return (xed_state_get_machine_mode(p) == XED_MACHINE_MODE_LEGACY_16) ||
        (xed_state_get_machine_mode(p) == XED_MACHINE_MODE_LONG_COMPAT_16);
}


static inline xed_bool_t xed_state_mode_width_32(const xed_state_t* p) {
    return (xed_state_get_machine_mode(p) == XED_MACHINE_MODE_LEGACY_32) ||
        (xed_state_get_machine_mode(p) == XED_MACHINE_MODE_LONG_COMPAT_32);
}




static inline void xed_state_set_machine_mode( xed_state_t* p,
                        xed_machine_mode_enum_t arg_mode) {
    p->mmode = arg_mode;
}







static inline xed_address_width_enum_t
xed_state_get_address_width(const xed_state_t* p)
{
    switch(xed_state_get_machine_mode(p)) {
      case XED_MACHINE_MODE_LONG_64:
        return XED_ADDRESS_WIDTH_64b;

      case XED_MACHINE_MODE_REAL_16:
      case XED_MACHINE_MODE_REAL_32:



        return XED_ADDRESS_WIDTH_32b;

      case XED_MACHINE_MODE_LEGACY_32:
      case XED_MACHINE_MODE_LONG_COMPAT_32:
        return XED_ADDRESS_WIDTH_32b;
      case XED_MACHINE_MODE_LEGACY_16:
      case XED_MACHINE_MODE_LONG_COMPAT_16:
        return XED_ADDRESS_WIDTH_16b;
      default:
        return XED_ADDRESS_WIDTH_INVALID;
    }
}







static inline void
xed_state_set_stack_address_width(xed_state_t* p,
                                  xed_address_width_enum_t arg_addr_width)
{
    p->stack_addr_width = arg_addr_width;
}




static inline xed_address_width_enum_t xed_state_get_stack_address_width(const xed_state_t* p) {
    return p->stack_addr_width;
}



__attribute__((visibility("default"))) int xed_state_print(const xed_state_t* p, char* buf, int buflen);

# 634 "/mnt/data/Projects/bdclient/coverage/pin-3.21-98484-ge7cd811fd-gcc-linux/extras/xed-intel64/include/xed/xed-encoder-hl.h"
static inline void xed_inst(
    xed_encoder_instruction_t* inst,
    xed_state_t mode,
    xed_iclass_enum_t iclass,
    xed_uint_t effective_operand_width,
    xed_uint_t number_of_operands,
    const xed_encoder_operand_t* operand_array) {

    xed_uint_t i;
    inst->mode=mode;
    inst->iclass = iclass;
    inst->effective_operand_width = effective_operand_width;
    inst->effective_address_width = 0;
    inst->prefixes.i = 0;
    do { } while(0);
    for(i=0;i<number_of_operands;i++) {
        inst->operands[i] = operand_array[i];
    }
    inst->noperands = number_of_operands;
}

# 308 "/mnt/data/Projects/bdclient/coverage/pin-3.21-98484-ge7cd811fd-gcc-linux/extras/xed-intel64/include/xed/xed-decoded-inst-api.h"
static inline xed_uint_t
xed_decoded_inst_get_machine_mode_bits(const xed_decoded_inst_t* p) {
    xed_uint_t mode = xed3_operand_get_mode(p);
    if (mode == 2) return 64;
    if (mode == 1) return 32;
    return 16;
}



static inline xed_uint_t
xed_decoded_inst_get_stack_address_mode_bits(const xed_decoded_inst_t* p) {
    xed_uint_t smode = xed3_operand_get_smode(p);
    if (smode == 2) return 64;
    if (smode == 1) return 32;
    return 16;
}

# 12 "instrument.c" 2







struct hsearch_data unpacker_modules;

typedef struct {
    uintptr_t address;
    size_t size;
    uint32_t count;
} execution_record_t;

int compare(const void *a, const void *b)
{
    const execution_record_t *x = a, *y = b;
    return x->address - y->address;
}

    }

    blocks = ep->data;

    static execution_record_t zero, *hblock = &zero;
    void **data;

    execution_record_t *record, block = {
        .address = address,
        .size = size,
        .count = 0,
    };


    if (hblock->address == address) {
        hblock->count++;
        return;
    }


    if (tree_find(blocks, &block, &data)) {
        record = *data;
    } else {

        record = malloc(sizeof(execution_record_t));
        memcpy(record, &block, sizeof(execution_record_t));
        tree_add(blocks, record, &data);
    }


    if (record->count++ >= hblock->count) {
        hblock = record;
    }

    return;
}


static const char kCoverageReport[] = "coverage.txt";
static const char kCoverageVariable[] = "COVERAGE_REPORT_FILE";

const execution_record_t *hblock = 
# 88 "instrument.c" 3 4
                                  ((void *)0)
# 88 "instrument.c"
                                      ;
unsigned instructions = 0;
unsigned blockcount = 0;
unsigned totalinstructions = 0;
unsigned totalblocks = 0;

void calculate_block_stats(const void *v) {
    const execution_record_t *d = v;
    blockcount++;
    instructions += d->size;
    totalblocks += d->count;
    totalinstructions += d->size * d->count;

    if (hblock == 
# 101 "instrument.c" 3 4
                 ((void *)0) 
# 101 "instrument.c"
                      || hblock->count < d->count)
        hblock = d;
}

VOID instrument_fini_callback(INT32 code, VOID *v)
{
    FILE *output = fopen(getenv(kCoverageVariable)
                            ? getenv(kCoverageVariable)
                            : kCoverageReport, "wx");

    void print_basic_blocks(const void *v) {
        register uintptr_t address = ((const execution_record_t *)(v))->address;
        fprintf(output, "%#010" 
# 113 "instrument.c" 3 4
                               "l""x" 
# 113 "instrument.c"
                                       "\n", address);
    }

    if (output != 
# 116 "instrument.c" 3 4
                 ((void *)0)
# 116 "instrument.c"
                     ) {
        tree_walk(blocks, print_basic_blocks);
    }

    tree_walk(blocks, calculate_block_stats);
    fprintf(
# 121 "instrument.c" 3 4
           (&__sF[2])
# 121 "instrument.c"
                 , "\n\n----- COVERAGE ANALYSIS -----\n");
    fprintf(
# 122 "instrument.c" 3 4
           (&__sF[2])
# 122 "instrument.c"
                 , "\t%10u Unique Instructions Executed\n", instructions);
    fprintf(
# 123 "instrument.c" 3 4
           (&__sF[2])
# 123 "instrument.c"
                 , "\t%10u Unique Basic Blocks Executed\n", blockcount);
    fprintf(
# 124 "instrument.c" 3 4
           (&__sF[2])
# 124 "instrument.c"
                 , "\t%10u Total Instructions Executed\n", totalinstructions);
    fprintf(
# 125 "instrument.c" 3 4
           (&__sF[2])
# 125 "instrument.c"
                 , "\t%10u Total Basic Blocks Executed\n", totalblocks);

    if (hblock) {
        fprintf(
# 128 "instrument.c" 3 4
               (&__sF[2])
# 128 "instrument.c"
                     , "\tHottest Basic Block (%#018" 
# 128 "instrument.c" 3 4
                                                      "l""x" 
# 128 "instrument.c"
                                                              ")\n", hblock->address);
        fprintf(
# 129 "instrument.c" 3 4
               (&__sF[2])
# 129 "instrument.c"
                     , "\t\t%10u Executes\n", hblock->count);
        fprintf(
# 130 "instrument.c" 3 4
               (&__sF[2])
# 130 "instrument.c"
                     , "\t\t%10zu Instructions\n", hblock->size);
    }

    tree_destroy(blocks);

    if (output) {
        fclose(output);
    }

    return;
}
